make our life easier. To enable this, we have 2 options: using key-based authentication by copying our SSH public keys to the remote machines for automatic password-less login or using password-based authentication. I will introduce the 2 options in the post. Before you <a href=\"https://www.systutorials.com/tag/start/\">start</a>, please note that key-based authentication is generally suggested when your working environment allows.</p><div id=\"st-in-post-1\"><span id=\"ezoic-pub-ad-placeholder-117\"></span><span style=\"display:inline-block;float:none;margin-bottom:2px !important;margin-left:0px !important;margin-right:0px !important;margin-top:2px !important;min-height:300px;min-width:336px;\" class=\"ezoic-ad box-3 adtester-container adtester-container-117\"><span id=\"div-gpt-ad-systutorials_com-box-3-0\" ezaw=\"336\" ezah=\"280\" style=\"position: relative; z-index: 0; min-height: 280px; min-width: 336px;\" class=\"ezoic-ad\" data-google-query-id=\"CLK_vJSvt9MCFVOMaQodP_sENQ\"><div id=\"google_ads_iframe_/1254144/systutorials_com-box-3_0__container__\" style=\"border: 0pt none; display: inline-block; width: 336px; height: 280px;\"><iframe frameborder=\"0\" src=\"https://tpc.googlesyndication.com/safeframe/1-0-8/html/container.html#eid=21060248,21060231\" id=\"google_ads_iframe_/1254144/systutorials_com-box-3_0\" title=\"3rd party ad content\" name=\"\" scrolling=\"no\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" width=\"336\" height=\"280\" data-is-safeframe=\"true\" style=\"border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom;\"></iframe></div></span></span></div><div class=\"align-center image-align-center\"><a href=\"https://www.systutorials.com/136968/three-methods-execute-commands-many-nodes-parallel-ssh-linux/ssh-terminal/\" rel=\"attachment\" title=\"ssh-terminal.png\"><img class=\"wp-post-image\" src=\"//www.systutorials.com.hub.hk/wp/files/2016/01/ssh-terminal.png\" title=\"ssh-terminal.png\" alt=\"ssh-terminal.png\" width=\"630\" height=\"393\"></a></div><h2 id=\"key-based-password-less-ssh-login\">Key-based password-less ssh login <a class=\"heading-link\" href=\"#key-based-password-less-ssh-login\" title=\"Link to this section\"></a></h2><p>We introduce two methods in this post: using <em>ssh-copy-id</em> <a href=\"https://www.systutorials.com/tag/command/\">command</a> and the manual way.</p><h3>Generate SSH key pair</h3><p>If you do not have a SSH private/public key pair yet, you can generate one first.</p><pre class=\"hljs ruby\">$ ssh-keygen -t rsa</pre><p>By default on <a href=\"https://www.systutorials.com/category/tutorial/linux/\">Linux</a>, the key pair is stored in <code class=\"not-hl\">~/.ssh</code> named <code class=\"not-hl\">id_rsa</code> and <code class=\"not-hl\">id_rsa.pub</code> for the private and public key.</p><h3>Copy public SSH key to the remote machine</h3><p>You have two choices here. Unless that you can not use the <code class=\"not-hl\">ssh-copy-id</code> method, you can try the manual way.</p><h4>The easiest way</h4><p>Let ssh-copy-id do it automatically:</p><pre class=\"hljs objectivec\">$ ssh-<span class=\"hljs-keyword\">copy</span>-<span class=\"hljs-keyword\">id</span> username@remotemachine</pre><p>If you have multiple keys in your <code class=\"not-hl\">~/.ssh</code> directory, you may need to use <code class=\"not-hl\">-i key_file</code> to specify which key you will use.</p><h4>The manual way</h4><p>Copy the public SSH key to remote machine</p><pre class=\"hljs ruby\">$ scp .ssh/id_rsa.pub username@remotemachine<span class=\"hljs-symbol\">:/tmp/</span></pre><p>Log on the remote machine</p><pre class=\"hljs ruby\">$ ssh username@remotemachine</pre><p>Append your public SSH key to <em>~/.ssh/authorized_keys</em></p><pre class=\"hljs ruby\"><span class=\"hljs-comment\"># backing up before changing is a good habit</span>\n$ cp ~<span class=\"hljs-regexp\">/.ssh/authorized</span>_keys ~<span class=\"hljs-regexp\">/.ssh/authorized</span>_keys.bak\n<span class=\"hljs-comment\"># append pub key to authorized keys list</span>\n$ cat /dev/shm/id_rsa.pub <span class=\"hljs-meta\">&gt;&gt; </span>~<span class=\"hljs-regexp\">/.ssh/authorized</span>_keys\n</pre><p>Make sure the mode of ~/.ssh/authorized_keys is 755:</p><pre class=\"hljs ruby\">$ chmod <span class=\"hljs-number\">755</span> ~<span class=\"hljs-regexp\">/.ssh/authorized</span>_keys</pre><h3>Possible Problems</h3><p>Some possible problems that prevent you from successfully setting up password-less login.</p><h4>Directory/file permissions</h4><p><strong>Home directory</strong><br> Check the home directorys permission which may cause the key-based login fail (suppose the home directory is /home/zma):</p><pre class=\"hljs apache\"><span class=\"hljs-comment\"># chmod 700 /home/zma/</span></pre><p><strong>~/.ssh permission</strong><br> Make sure the .ssh directorys permission is 755:</p><pre class=\"hljs ruby\">$ chmod <span class=\"hljs-number\">755</span> ~<span class=\"hljs-regexp\">/.ssh/</span></pre><p><strong>~/.ssh/authroized_keys permission</strong><br> Make sure the .ssh directorys permission is 755:</p><pre class=\"hljs ruby\">$ chmod <span class=\"hljs-number\">755</span> ~<span class=\"hljs-regexp\">/.ssh/authorized</span>_keys</pre><p><strong>~/.ssh/id_rsa and ~/.ssh/id_rsa.pub permission</strong><br> Make sure the permission is 700 (others can work, but 700 is better for your private key, right?):</p><pre class=\"hljs ruby\">$ chmod <span class=\"hljs-number\">700</span> ~<span class=\"hljs-regexp\">/.ssh/id</span>_rsa\n$ chmod <span class=\"hljs-number\">700</span> ~<span class=\"hljs-regexp\">/.ssh/id</span>_rsa.pub</pre><h2 id=\"password-based-.22password-less.22-ssh-login\">Password-based password-less ssh login <a class=\"heading-link\" href=\"#password-based-.22password-less.22-ssh-login\" title=\"Link to this section\"></a></h2><p>This method the login and authentication is still by password. However, we use a tool to help us input the password automatically. The tool is <a class=\"external external-man\" href=\"https://www.systutorials.com/docs/linux/man/1-sshpass/\"><code class=\"not-hl\">sshpass</code></a> which works nicely.</p><p>The usage is very simple as follows by providing the password in command line:</p><pre class=\"code not-hl hljs ruby\">$ sshpass -p <span class=\"hljs-string\">\"your_password_here\"</span> ssh username@remotemachine</pre><p>or by providing the password in the first line of a file</p><pre class=\"code not-hl hljs ruby\">$ sshpass -f /path/to/file_storing_your_password ssh username@remotemachine</pre><p>Security considerations: before using the <code class=\"not-hl\">sshpass</code>, please read the SECURITY CONSIDERATIONS section of the <a class=\"external external-man\" href=\"https://www.systutorials.com/docs/linux/man/1-sshpass/\"><code class=\"not-hl\">sshpass</code> man page</a> to know the security problems and only use it when you can tolerate them.</p><div style=\"margin-bottom:1em;\"><div class=\"the_champ_counter_container the_champ_horizontal_counter\" ss-offset=\"0\"><ul class=\"the_champ_sharing_ul\"><li
